Gedeeld met Openbare groep

THE PEER to PEER SIDE HUSTLE EFFECT (or CAMPLIFY / INFLUENCER EFFECT)
True backpacker campervans are coming back in prices and are now
appearing on this page (under $10K).
Still there are many vans that are beautifully fitted out with what
appear to be brand new fit outs and BIG asking prices.... Who is
building them and why? Who is buying them and why?
The people building them are building them because they are making good
money flipping them or at least that's their plan.
The people buying them are punters who think they're going to run a 1 or
more vans as a side hustle by renting them on peer to peer sites, or
they're influencers who need a van for their #vanlife content. Consider
them 'investors'. These investors are the people pushing up the prices,
it's not a COVID TAX and it's not a supply issue.
Just like AirBnB is a pox on the rental market, forcing up rents all
around the country, so is Camplify.
